The Company reported GAAP earnings per share (EPS) from continuing operations of $1.16</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">in third quarter 2018, up 33.6</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">percent from $0.87 in third quarter 2017. The attached tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP to GAAP measures. All earnings per share figures refer to diluted EPS.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8211; more &#8211;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><div style="padding-left:0px;text-indent:0px;line-height:normal;padding-top:10px;"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;"><tr><td colspan="1"></td></tr><tr><td style="width:100%;"></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;border-top:1px solid #000000;"><div style="overflow:hidden;height:5px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="padding-bottom:4px;font-size:7pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:7pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:5pt">1 </sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:7pt;">Adjusted EPS, a non-GAAP financial measure, excludes the impact of certain discretely managed items. We plan to leverage our current momentum into 2019, when we&#8217;ll achieve greater scale across the full slate of our initiatives - creating efficiencies and cost-savings, further strengthening our guest experience and positioning Target for profitable growth in the years ahead.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Fourth Quarter and Full-Year 2018 Guidance</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">For the fourth quarter, Target expects comparable sales growth of approximately 5 percent, consistent with the Company&#8217;s year-to-date performance through third quarter 2018. For the full year, the Company continues to expect Adjusted EPS of $5.30 to $5.50 and GAAP EPS of $5.41 to $5.61. The 11-cent difference between expected full-year Adjusted EPS and GAAP EPS is driven by discrete items already reported through third quarter 2018.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The Company announced today that it plans to issue a post-holiday financial update on Thursday, January 10, 2019.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Operating Results</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Total revenue of $17.8 billion increased 5.6 percent from $16.9</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">billion last year, reflecting sales growth of 5.7</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">percent and other revenue growth of 1.6</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">percent. Third quarter sales growth included a 5.1 percent increase in comparable sales and a 0.6 percentage point contribution from non-mature stores.  Comparable digital channel sales grew 49 percent and contributed 1.9</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">percentage points of comparable sales growth.  Operating income was $819</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">million in third quarter 2018, down 3.3 percent from $847</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">million in 2017.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8211; more &#8211;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><br></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;">Target Corporation Reports Third Quarter 2018 Earnings - Page 3 of 13</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Third quarter operating income margin rate was 4.6 percent, compared with 5.0 percent in 2017. Third quarter gross margin rate was 28.7 percent, compared with 29.6 percent in 2017. This decline reflected higher supply chain costs driven by growth in digital fulfillment costs and other expenses related to the size and timing of holiday-related inventory receipts compared with last year, partially offset by the benefit of merchant initiatives. Third quarter SG&amp;A expense rate was 22.1 percent in 2018, essentially flat to last year. Third quarter SG&amp;A results reflected continued investments in our team, specifically hours, training and wages, which were offset by continued cost discipline across the enterprise. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Interest Expense and Taxes from Continuing Operations</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">The Company&#8217;s third quarter 2018 net interest expense was $115 million, down 54.1</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">percent from $251</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">million last year, primarily driven by early debt retirement costs recognized in third quarter last year. Third quarter 2018 effective income tax rate from continuing operations was 13.6 percent, compared with 22.2 percent last year. Third quarter 2018 effective income tax rate from continuing operations reflects the net tax effect of the federal tax reform legislation (the Tax Act), including both ongoing and discrete benefits. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Capital Deployment</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">In third quarter 2018 the Company made capital investments of $1,017 million in property and equipment, and returned $863 million to shareholders, including:</font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:96px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:174%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:72px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Dividends of $337</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">million, compared with $339</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">million in third quarter 2017, reflecting a decline in share count partially offset by an increase in the dividend per share.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="padding-bottom:13px;font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:96px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:174%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:72px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Share repurchases totaling $526</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">million that retired 6.3</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">million shares of common stock at an average price of $84.00. </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">As of the end of the third quarter, the Company had approximately $1.8</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">billion of remaining capacity under its current $5 billion share repurchase program, reflecting third quarter purchases and an accelerated share repurchase transaction which will settle in the fourth quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8211; more &#8211;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><br></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;">Target Corporation Reports Third Quarter 2018 Earnings - Page 4 of 13</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">For the trailing twelve months through third quarter 2018, after-tax return on invested capital (ROIC) was 15.8</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">percent, compared with 13.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;color:#ff0000;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">percent for the twelve months through third quarter 2017. Excluding the discrete impacts of the Tax Act, ROIC was 13.9 percent for the trailing twelve months ended November 3, 2018.  See the tables of this release for additional information about the Company&#8217;s ROIC calculation.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call Details</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;padding-bottom:13px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">Target will webcast its third quarter earnings conference call at 7:00 a.m. CST today. These measures are not in accordance with, or an alternative for, GAAP. The most comparable GAAP measure is net earnings from continuing operations. EBIT and EBITDA should not be considered in isolation or as a substitution for analysis of our results as reported under GAAP. Other companies may calculate EBIT and EBITDA differently, limiting the usefulness of the measure for comparisons with other companies. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><div
